namespace ElmSharp
{
    /// <summary>
    /// A class that contains extension methods to wrap events for classes contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp"/> namespace.
    /// </summary>
    public static class EventExtensions
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static ButtonEvents Events(this ElmSharp.Button item) => new ButtonEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Calendar"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static CalendarEvents Events(this ElmSharp.Calendar item) => new CalendarEvents(item);

    /// <summary>
    /// A class which wraps the events contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button"/> class as observables.
    /// </summary>
    public class ButtonEvents
    {
        private readonly ElmSharp.Button _data;
        /// <summary>
        /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name = "data">The class that is being wrapped.</param>
        public ButtonEvents(ElmSharp.Button data)
        {
            _data = data;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets an observable which signals when the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button.Clicked"/> event triggers.
        /// </summary>
        public System.IObservable<System.EventArgs> Clicked => System.Reactive.Linq.Observable.FromEventPattern<System.EventHandler, System.EventArgs>(x => _data.Clicked += x, x => _data.Clicked -= x).Select(x => x.EventArgs);
        /// <summary>
        /// Gets an observable which signals when the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button.Pressed"/> event triggers.
        /// </summary>
        public System.IObservable<System.EventArgs> Pressed => System.Reactive.Linq.Observable.FromEventPattern<System.EventHandler, System.EventArgs>(x => _data.Pressed += x, x => _data.Pressed -= x).Select(x => x.EventArgs);
        /// <summary>
        /// Gets an observable which signals when the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button.Released"/> event triggers.
        /// </summary>
        public System.IObservable<System.EventArgs> Released => System.Reactive.Linq.Observable.FromEventPattern<System.EventHandler, System.EventArgs>(x => _data.Released += x, x => _data.Released -= x).Select(x => x.EventArgs);
        /// <summary>
        /// Gets an observable which signals when the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Button.Repeated"/> event triggers.
        /// </summary>
        public System.IObservable<System.EventArgs> Repeated => System.Reactive.Linq.Observable.FromEventPattern<System.EventHandler, System.EventArgs>(x => _data.Repeated += x, x => _data.Repeated -= x).Select(x => x.EventArgs);
    }

namespace ElmSharp.Wearable
{
    /// <summary>
    /// A class that contains extension methods to wrap events for classes contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Wearable"/> namespace.
    /// </summary>
    public static class EventExtensions
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Wearable.CircleSlider"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static CircleSliderEvents Events(this ElmSharp.Wearable.CircleSlider item) => new CircleSliderEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Wearable.MoreOption"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static MoreOptionEvents Events(this ElmSharp.Wearable.MoreOption item) => new MoreOptionEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Wearable.RotarySelector"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static RotarySelectorEvents Events(this ElmSharp.Wearable.RotarySelector item) => new RotarySelectorEvents(item);
    }

        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.Window"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static WindowEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.Window item) => new WindowEvents(item);
    }

namespace Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents
{
    /// <summary>
    /// A class that contains extension methods to wrap events for classes contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents"/> namespace.
    /// </summary>
    public static class EventExtensions
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.ImageView"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static ImageViewEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.ImageView item) => new ImageViewEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.Scrollable"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static ScrollableEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.Scrollable item) => new ScrollableEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.TextEditor"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static TextEditorEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.TextEditor item) => new TextEditorEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.TextField"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static TextFieldEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.TextField item) => new TextFieldEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.VideoView"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static VideoViewEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.VideoView item) => new VideoViewEvents(item);
        /// <summary>
        /// A wrapper class which wraps all the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.View"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        public static ViewEvents Events(this Tizen.NUI.BaseComponents.View item) => new ViewEvents(item);
    }

    /// A class which wraps the events contained within the <see cref = "Tizen.Sensor.Accelerometer"/> class as observables.
    /// </summary>
    public class AccelerometerEvents
    {
        private readonly Tizen.Sensor.Accelerometer _data;
        /// <summary>
        /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref = "Tizen.Sensor.Accelerometer"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name = "data">The class that is being wrapped.</param>
        public AccelerometerEvents(Tizen.Sensor.Accelerometer data)
        {
            _data = data;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets an observable which signals when the <see cref = "Tizen.Sensor.Accelerometer.DataUpdated"/> event triggers.
        /// </summary>
        public System.IObservable<Tizen.Sensor.AccelerometerDataUpdatedEventArgs> DataUpdated => System.Reactive.Linq.Observable.FromEventPattern<System.EventHandler<Tizen.Sensor.AccelerometerDataUpdatedEventArgs>, Tizen.Sensor.AccelerometerDataUpdatedEventArgs>(x => _data.DataUpdated += x, x => _data.DataUpdated -= x).Select(x => x.EventArgs);
    }

namespace ElmSharp.Wearable
{
    /// <summary>
    /// A class that contains extension methods to wrap events contained within static classes within the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Wearable"/> namespace.
    /// </summary>
    public static class Events
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Gets an observable which signals when the <see cref = "ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventManager.Rotated"/> event triggers.
        /// </summary>
        public static System.IObservable<ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventArgs> RotaryEventManagerRotated => System.Reactive.Linq.Observable.FromEvent<ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventHandler, ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventArgs>(eventHandler =>
        {
            void Handler(ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventArgs args) => eventHandler(args);
            return Handler;
        }

        , x => ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventManager.Rotated += x, x => ElmSharp.Wearable.RotaryEventManager.Rotated -= x);
    }
}
